##### ![](https://media.phish.net/avatars/default_avatar.png)Phish.net

[Phish.net](https://phish.net/) is a non-commercial project run by Phish fans and for Phish fans under the auspices of the all-volunteer, non-profit Mockingbird Foundation.

This project serves to compile, preserve, and protect encyclopedic information about Phish and their music.

[Credits](https://phish.net/credits) \| [Terms Of Use](https://phish.net/page/terms-of-use) \| [Legal](https://phish.net/page/legal) \| [DMCA](https://phish.net/page/dmca)

##### Donate to Mockingbird

[Make a Donation](https://donate.mbird.org/np/clients/mbird/donation.jsp)

##### Contact Us

[Click here to contact us](https://phish.net/contact)

##### ![](https://media.phish.net/site/socialmedia/mbird.png)The Mockingbird Foundation

[The Mockingbird Foundation](https://mbird.org/) is a non-profit organization founded by Phish fans in 1996 to generate charitable proceeds from the Phish community.

And since we're **entirely volunteer** – with no office, salaries, or paid staff – administrative costs are less than 2% of revenues! So far, we've distributed over $2 million to support music education for children – hundreds of grants in all 50 states, with more on the way.

© 1990-2025  The Mockingbird Foundation, Inc.
